<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шастать.html>ша́стать</a> (12985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шастать.html>ша́стать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šástatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roam, to hang about, to hang around</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***шатать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́ть</a> (26756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">шатати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šatati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šętati</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">шѩтаниѥ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šjętanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">шата́тися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šatátysja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sway, to stagger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ше́там</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šétam</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go back and forth, to manage, to serve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ше́тати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ше̑та̄м</i> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ше̑ће̄м</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">šétati se</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">šátat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šatátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зашата́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шатну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sway, to rock, to shake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>Брат</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кивать.html>кива́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухмыляться.html>ухмыля́лся</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ного́ю</a> лёгкий <a href = vnd.unilang:тазик.html>та́зик</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Brat na éto kivál i uxmyljálsja, <b>šatája</b> nogóju ljóxkij tázik</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My brother beckoned and grinned at it, <b>swaying</b> with his foot the tranquil basin</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sway; to (cause to) stagger, to (cause to) reel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šatájet</b> mužčínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the man is <b>staggering</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шататься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шататься.html>шата́ться</a> (6736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шататься.html>шата́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šatátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зашататься.html>зашата́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатнуться.html>шатну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sway, to rock, to shake; to stagger, to reel; to be unstable</li>
<li>to lounge, to roam, to loaf about</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатать.html>шата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šatátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language, also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">çadër</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu">sátor</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurdish_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Kurdish languages">Kurdish</a></span> <i class="ku-Arab mention" lang="ku">چادر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ku-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">çadir</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">چادر</i> | , <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">šator</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">çadır</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urdu" class="extiw" title="w:Urdu">Urdu</a></span> <i class="ur-Arab mention" lang="ur">چادر</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ur-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ćādar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатёр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šatjór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>large tent <i>(portable lodge)</i>, marquee
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Е. П. Карнович, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высоте́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доля.html>до́ле</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:царевна.html>Царе́вна</a> Софья Алексеевна</i> 1879:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приятный.html>прия́тный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:послеобеденный.html>послеобе́денный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сон</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боярин.html>боя́рина</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внезапно.html>внеза́пно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прерванный.html>пре́рван</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шу́мом</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поднявшийся.html>подня́вшимся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:около.html>о́коло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шатер.html>шатра́</a></b></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijátnyj posleobédennyj son bojárina byl vnezápno prérvan šúmom, podnjavšimsja ókolo jevó <b>šatrá</b></i></dd><dd>the pleasing postprandial sleep of the boyar was suddenly interrupted by noise from near his <b>tent</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hipped roof, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tented_roof" class="extiw" title="w:tented roof">tented roof</a></li></ol>

***шаткий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаткий.html>ша́ткий</a> (14709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шат(а́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šat(átʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаткий.html>ша́ткий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šátkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ша́тче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shaky, unsteady, rickety</li>
<li>precarious, wavering, weak, unsteady
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шаткий.html>ша́ткое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šátkoje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">precarious/shaky position</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаткий.html>ша́тко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> ва́лко</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni šátko ni válko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) neither good nor bad; middling well; 2) slowly; at a snail's pace</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахматы.html>ша́хматы</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šaxmaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schāch unde <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schachmatt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">checkmate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">شاه مات</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šâh mât</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the king is conquered</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***шахта.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хта</a> (4837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">schacht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šáxta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mine, pit (place from which ore is extracted)</li>
<li>shaft</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шахтный.html>ша́хтный</a> (29581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахта.html>ша́хта</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šáxta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шахтный.html>ша́хтный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šáxtnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">underground tunnel for extracting ore</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шахтный.html>ша́хтное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборудование.html>обору́дование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šáxtnoje</b> oborúdovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mine</b> equipment</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shaft, mine shaft</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> furnished with a shaft, shafted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шахтный.html>ша́хтная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>šáxtnaja</b> pečʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>shafted</b> oven</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шашка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шка</a> (7366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шах.html>шах</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šax</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">check</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šáška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>checker, draughtsman <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a piece in a game of checkers/draughts</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> checkers/draughts <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">board game</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>explosive charge, stick <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of dynamite</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> smoke grenade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">construction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paving block</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif/lossy-page1-150px-Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif/lossy-page1-225px-Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif/lossy-page1-300px-Sabel%2C_schaschka_-_Livrustkammaren_-_1315_%28cropped%29.tif.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2776" data-file-height="4700" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:кавказский.html>Кавка́зская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шка</a></div></div></div>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circassian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Circassian languages">Circassian</a></span> borrowing, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adyghe_language" class="extiw" title="w:Adyghe language">Adyghe</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ady">сэшхуэ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ady-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">săšx°ă</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">long knife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šáška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cossack sabre, Circassian sabre, shashka <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a type of guardless, lightly-curved sabre</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rider, cavalryman <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as a counting unit of military strength</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> 6200 <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыко́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> 1500 <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шашка.html>ша́шек</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> 20 <a href = vnd.unilang:орудие.html>ору́диях</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U protívnika 6200 štykóv i 1500 <b>šášek</b> pri 20 orúdijax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The adversary has 6200 infantry and 1500 <b>cavalry</b> supported by 20 pieces of artillery</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crimean_Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Crimean Tatar language">Crimean Tatar</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="crh">şışlıq</i> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="crh">шишлик</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шваль.html>шваль</a> (28139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Sometimes compared with German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schwall</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cheval</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шваль.html>шваль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">švalʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шваль.html>шва́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шваль.html>шва́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шваль.html>шва́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes collectively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scum, dregs, despicable person, riffraff, despicable people</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually collectively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rubbish, useless things</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***швед.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:швед.html>швед</a> (10425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schwede</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швед.html>швед</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šved</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швед.html>шве́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швед.html>шве́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швед.html>шве́дов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шве́дка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Swede (Swedish person)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шве́ция</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Švécija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">шве́дка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">švédka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***швейцар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:швейцар.html>швейца́р</a> (7803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schweizer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Swiss person; doorman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (because Swiss people were often employed as doormen), possibly via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szwajcar</i>. First used in the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейцар.html>швейца́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">švejcár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейцар.html>швейца́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейцар.html>швейца́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейцар.html>швейца́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>doorman (doorkeeper, usher, porter)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Swiss man</li></ol>

***швырнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:швырнуть.html>швырну́ть</a> (4053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырнуть.html>швырну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">švyrnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырять.html>швыря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to toss, to hurl, to throw, to chuck</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put things in disorder, to not where they belong (e.g. clothing)</li>
<li>to fling (money)</li></ol>

***швырять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:швырять.html>швыря́ть</a> (7367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырнуть.html>швырну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">švyrnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырять.html>швыря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">švyrjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырнуть.html>швырну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to toss, to hurl, to throw, to chuck</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put things in disorder, to not where they belong (e.g. clothing)</li>
<li>to fling (money)</li></ol>
